warning: use of deprecated method `ecs::query::QueryState::<Q, F>::iter`: Use `CachedArchetypeQueryState` instead for 
zero-allocation, cache-friendly iteration. This method allocates a new Vec every call and iterates the entire 
`entity_components` HashMap with binary search, resulting in ~95% slower performance. 
         Migration example:
         Before: `let state = QueryState::<&Position>::new(); for (e, pos) in state.iter(&world) { ... }`
         After:  `let mut query = CachedArchetypeQueryState::<&Position>::new(); for (e, pos) in query.iter(&world) { 
... }`
